    </div>      </div>      <div class="article-content">          <!-- Lead Media -->                        <div class="component video lead-media ">              <span hidden class="jumpstart-video-data" data-jumpstart-version="v3"></span>                <div class="jumpstart-video">                  <video class="video-js" data-embed="default" data-controls="true"                   data-account="2157889318001"                  data-player="default"                  data-brand="si"                  data-video-id="5752826171001"                                                                           poster="https://cdn-s3.si.com/styles/marquee_large_2x/s3/images/5ab3a402197e8a0b2f00000f.jpg?itok&#x3D;3q7qxnG0"                  data-autoplay="true"                  data-viewplay="true"                  data-stickyplay="true"                                    data-is-lead="true"></video>                </div>            </div>            <p class="dek margin-24-tb padded-mobile">              From Messi's single-season dominance to the fastest goal in Premier League history, here are some marks that we're unlikely to ever see fall.                        </p>          <!-- Author and Date -->          <div class="author scale-12 padded margin-24-tb clearfix">            <div class="author-text" data-tracking-zone="author">                    By                                     <a class="bold author-name" href="/people/90-min">90Min</a>                              <div class="timestamp published-date padding-12-left">                      March 22, 2018                    </div>            </div>          </div>        <!-- Article Content -->        <div id="article-body" class="article content body clearfix" data-tracking-zone="body">          <div class="padded">                <p data-label="Drop here...">Records are made to be broken, or so the old saying goes anyway. While that often rings true, there are occasional feats of brilliance that set benchmarks so high, it becomes near impossible to better them.</p>                <p data-label="Drop here...">Here, we take a look at seven footballing records, that despite the efforts of many of the world's best, will prove near impossible to overhaul in the years to come.</p>                <hr>                <p><b>Fastest Premier League Goal </b></p>                <p><b>Ledley King (Tottenham Hotspur) - 9.9 seconds</b></p>                <div class="component inline image margin-16-top margin-24-bottom">                  <div class="image-wrapper">                    <div                      class="component lazy-image                           no-upscale                                                                         "                      data-src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aaba037da7e234fae000001.jpeg"                      data-alt=""                                                                  >                                            <noscript>                        <div class="inner-container">                          <img src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aaba037da7e234fae000001.jpeg" alt="">                        </div>                      </noscript>                      <div class="inner-container js-inner-container">                      </div>                                              <div class="image-wrap-container clearfix">                          <div class="credit body-credit padding-8-top padding-8-bottom">Image by Toby Cudworth</div>                        </div>                    </div>                  </div>                </div>                <p data-label="Drop here...">Our first look at history takes us back to December 2000, when Tottenham Hotspur defender Ledley King notched the fastest goal in Premier League history.</p>                                <div                  id="ad-300x250_LL_m_1"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-300x250 instream-ad mobile-ad "                  data-dimensions="300x250"                  data-tgxtrack="true" data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxupdatecorrelator="true" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                                <div                  id="ad-728x90_LL_td_1"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-728x90 instream-ad tablet-ad desktop-ad "                  data-dimensions="728x90"                  data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                <p>Picking up a stray ball in the Bradford City half following kick off, the England international waltzed towards the edge of the penalty area, before rifling a deflected effort past Matt Clarke in the Bantams goal.</p>                <p>The goal was clocked at just 9.9 seconds, with efforts from Alan Shearer and Christian Eriksen the nearest challengers to a record that has now lasted over 17 years.</p>                <hr>                <p><a href="https://www.si.com/planetfutbolTV" target="_blank"><em>Watch Grant Wahl and Luis Miguel Echegaray provide expert soccer analysis every week on SI TV's Planet Fútbol show.</em></a></p>                <div class="full-width-media">                  <div class="media-item clearfix">                    <div align="center"><a href="https://aax-us-east.amazon-adsystem.com/x/c/QgA1CMx1Hn10o4-Ezv490dwAAAFh2JTxHQEAAAFKAefVMP8/https://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_at?creativeASIN=2858778011&amp;linkCode=w50&amp;tag=sportsillustrated0f-20&amp;imprToken=QWJlDqn5YSew32XEq7yobA&amp;slotNum=2&amp;_encoding=UTF8&amp;benefitId=sportsillustrated&amp;node=2858778011&amp;ref=DVM_US_JK_PS_SITVb2%7Cc_233136791014_m_zsYAlJoD-dc_s__" target="_blank"><img style="max-width: 100%;" alt="SI TV on Amazon channels" src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/s3fs-public/2018/02/27/si-tv-tout-final.png" /> </a></div>                  </div>                </div>                                <div                  id="ad-5x5_LL_mtd_2"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-5x5 instream-ad  "                  data-dimensions="5x5"                  data-tgxtrack="true" data-tgxtargeting="%7B%22tds%22%3A1%7D" data-tgxlazy="200"                >                </div>                <hr>                <p><strong>Record Attendance</strong></p>                <p><strong>Brazil vs Uruguay (1950 World Cup Final) 173,850</strong></p>                <div class="component inline image margin-16-top margin-24-bottom">                  <div class="image-wrapper">                    <div                      class="component lazy-image                           no-upscale                                                                         "                      data-src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aaba4b439e96e2731000001.jpeg"                      data-alt=""                                                                  >                                            <noscript>                        <div class="inner-container">                          <img src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aaba4b439e96e2731000001.jpeg" alt="">                        </div>                      </noscript>                      <div class="inner-container js-inner-container">                      </div>                                              <div class="image-wrap-container clearfix">                          <div class="credit body-credit padding-8-top padding-8-bottom">Image by Toby Cudworth</div>                        </div>                    </div>                  </div>                </div>                <p data-label="Drop here...">The conclusion of the most unique World Cup in history took place at the iconic Maracanã Stadium, as hosts Brazil hosted Uruguay in the deciding match of the 1950 tournament.</p>                                <div                  id="ad-300x250_LL_m_3"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-300x250 instream-ad mobile-ad "                  data-dimensions="300x250"                  data-tgxtrack="true" data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxupdatecorrelator="true" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                                <div                  id="ad-728x90_LL_td_3"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-728x90 instream-ad tablet-ad desktop-ad "                  data-dimensions="728x90"                  data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                <p data-label="Drop here...">Support throughout the tournament for Brazil had been nothing short of phenomenal, with the favorites playing in front of huge partisan crowds. Their showdown against Uruguay in the final group game would ultimately decide the destiny of the Jules Rimet trophy, with the home side coming into the game in imperious form.</p>                <p data-label="Drop here...">A staggering 173,850 spectators crammed in to witness the Samba kings coronation, though Uruguay's Alcides Ghiggia clearly didn't receive the memo, as he scored the goal to complete a stunning comeback for La Celeste in front of the largest crowd ever seen.</p>                <hr>                <p data-label="Drop here..."><strong>Longest Unbeaten Run</strong></p>                <p data-label="Drop here..."><strong>Steaua Bucharest (1986-89) 104 games</strong></p>                <div class="component inline image margin-16-top margin-24-bottom">                  <div class="image-wrapper">                    <div                      class="component lazy-image                           no-upscale                                                                         "                      data-src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aabb17b1d79cd1170000003.jpeg"                      data-alt=""                                                                  >                                            <noscript>                        <div class="inner-container">                          <img src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aabb17b1d79cd1170000003.jpeg" alt="">                        </div>                      </noscript>                      <div class="inner-container js-inner-container">                      </div>                                              <div class="image-wrap-container clearfix">                          <div class="credit body-credit padding-8-top padding-8-bottom">Image by Toby Cudworth</div>                        </div>                    </div>                  </div>                </div>                <p data-label="Drop here...">We've seen some fairly impressive unbeaten runs over the years, ranging from AC Milan's unbeaten run of 58 games between 1991 and 1993, to Arsenal's Invincibles in the 2003/04 Premier League season.</p>                                <div                  id="ad-300x250_LL_m_4"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-300x250 instream-ad mobile-ad "                  data-dimensions="300x250"                  data-tgxtrack="true" data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxupdatecorrelator="true" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                                <div                  id="ad-728x90_LL_td_4"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-728x90 instream-ad tablet-ad desktop-ad "                  data-dimensions="728x90"                  data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                <p data-label="Drop here...">Astoundingly, their impressive periods of sustained form pale into insignificance against the all conquering Steaua Bucharest side of the late 1980's. The Romanian heavyweights marked their territory on both the domestic and European scene, winning countless titles in an era of relentless dominance.</p>                <p data-label="Drop here...">In total, they went unbeaten in 104 games in Romania's Liga 1, with Steaua failing to taste defeat between June 1986 and September 1989 en route to scooping up a quadruple of league crowns.</p>                <hr>                <p data-label="Drop here..."><strong>Record Number of Goals in a Single Season</strong></p>                <p data-label="Drop here..."><strong>Lionel Messi (Barcelona) 73 goals</strong></p>                <div class="component inline image margin-16-top margin-24-bottom">                  <div class="image-wrapper">                    <div                      class="component lazy-image                           no-upscale                                                                         "                      data-src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aabb816197e8a1152000020.jpg"                      data-alt=""                                                                  >                                            <noscript>                        <div class="inner-container">                          <img src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aabb816197e8a1152000020.jpg" alt="">                        </div>                      </noscript>                      <div class="inner-container js-inner-container">                      </div>                                              <div class="image-wrap-container clearfix">                          <div class="credit body-credit padding-8-top padding-8-bottom">LLUIS GENE/GettyImages</div>                        </div>                    </div>                  </div>                </div>                <p data-label="Drop here...">Quite possibly the greatest footballer to ever walk the planet, Argentina's Lionel Messi at times seems like he's in a world of his own.</p>                                <div                  id="ad-300x250_LL_m_5"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-300x250 instream-ad mobile-ad "                  data-dimensions="300x250"                  data-tgxtrack="true" data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxupdatecorrelator="true" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                                <div                  id="ad-728x90_LL_td_5"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-728x90 instream-ad tablet-ad desktop-ad "                  data-dimensions="728x90"                  data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                <p data-label="Drop here...">There are no adequate superlatives to describe Messi's unbelievable ability, with any attempt likely to undermine his unwavering talent. In order to grasp just how good he is, you only need to look towards a swathe of impressive statistics.</p>                <p data-label="Drop here...">More specifically in the context of this list, we refer to his outstanding season back in 2011/12. Making 60 appearances over the course of the season, Barcelona's talisman notched an incredible 73 goals, easily surpassing a ratio of better than one goal per game.</p>                <p data-label="Drop here...">Such greatness has never been seen before, and may never be replicated again.</p>                <hr>                <p data-label="Drop here..."><strong>Record Aggregate Win</strong></p>                <p><strong>Benfica vs Stade Dudelange (1965-66) 18-0</strong></p>                <div class="component inline image margin-16-top margin-24-bottom">                  <div class="image-wrapper">                    <div                      class="component lazy-image                           no-upscale                                                                         "                      data-src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aabbbfa913da9d807000001.jpeg"                      data-alt=""                                                                  >                                            <noscript>                        <div class="inner-container">                          <img src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aabbbfa913da9d807000001.jpeg" alt="">                        </div>                      </noscript>                      <div class="inner-container js-inner-container">                      </div>                                              <div class="image-wrap-container clearfix">                          <div class="credit body-credit padding-8-top padding-8-bottom">Image by Toby Cudworth</div>                        </div>                    </div>                  </div>                </div>                <p data-label="Drop here...">European competition can occasionally pit together some significant forces against aspiring minnows, as qualification for the showpiece events of the year get underway.</p>                                <div                  id="ad-300x250_LL_m_6"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-300x250 instream-ad mobile-ad "                  data-dimensions="300x250"                  data-tgxtrack="true" data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxupdatecorrelator="true" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                                <div                  id="ad-728x90_LL_td_6"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-728x90 instream-ad tablet-ad desktop-ad "                  data-dimensions="728x90"                  data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                <p data-label="Drop here...">These clashes don't often go the way of the underdog, though none have been as one sided as Portuguese giants Benfica's clash against Luxembourg's Stade Dudelange during the 1965/66 season.</p>                <p data-label="Drop here...">Contested over two legs, Benfica showed a ruthless side never seen before, easing to 10-0 and 8-0 wins to wrap up a thoroughly comprehensive 18-0 aggregate win. Such a margin has not been since, and is unlikely to be seen again in the modern game.</p>                <hr>                <p><strong>Record Points Haul While Suffering Relegation From the Premier League</strong></p>                <p><strong>West Ham United (2002/03) 42 points</strong></p>                <div class="component inline image margin-16-top margin-24-bottom">                  <div class="image-wrapper">                    <div                      class="component lazy-image                           no-upscale                                                                         "                      data-src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aabc593c9c15a820b000005.jpg"                      data-alt=""                                                                  >                                            <noscript>                        <div class="inner-container">                          <img src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aabc593c9c15a820b000005.jpg" alt="">                        </div>                      </noscript>                      <div class="inner-container js-inner-container">                      </div>                                              <div class="image-wrap-container clearfix">                          <div class="credit body-credit padding-8-top padding-8-bottom">Ross Kinnaird/GettyImages</div>                        </div>                    </div>                  </div>                </div>                <p>The Premier League has seen some epic relegation tussles over the years, with this season's scrap at the bottom of the table shaping up to be another titanic slug fest.</p>                                <div                  id="ad-300x250_LL_m_7"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-300x250 instream-ad mobile-ad "                  data-dimensions="300x250"                  data-tgxtrack="true" data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxupdatecorrelator="true" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                                <div                  id="ad-728x90_LL_td_7"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-728x90 instream-ad tablet-ad desktop-ad "                  data-dimensions="728x90"                  data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                <p>One of the most memorable battles culminated in a final day showdown between Bolton Wanderers and West Ham United. Both teams headed into the final day's fixtures locked on 41 points; a record haul for any side facing the prospect of relegation.</p>                <p>Bolton would see off Middlesbrough at the Reebok Stadium, meaning the Hammers 2-2 draw at Birmingham would consign them to the Championship, toppling them out of the top flight with an astonishing 42 points.</p>                <div class="component page-break" data-page="1" data-title="7 World Soccer Records That Will Be Near Impossible to Break" data-template="article" data-path=""></div>                <hr>                <p><strong>Shortest Number of Games to Reach 300 La Liga Goals</strong></p>                <p data-label="Drop here..."><strong>Cristiano Ronaldo (2009-2018) 286 games</strong></p>                <div class="component inline image margin-16-top margin-24-bottom">                  <div class="image-wrapper">                    <div                      class="component lazy-image                           no-upscale                                                                         "                      data-src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aabc4cbda7e231e9c000003.jpg"                      data-alt=""                                                                  >                                            <noscript>                        <div class="inner-container">                          <img src="https://cdn-s3.si.com/images/5aabc4cbda7e231e9c000003.jpg" alt="">                        </div>                      </noscript>                      <div class="inner-container js-inner-container">                      </div>                                              <div class="image-wrap-container clearfix">                          <div class="credit body-credit padding-8-top padding-8-bottom">Juan Manuel Serrano Arce/GettyImages</div>                        </div>                    </div>                  </div>                </div>                <p data-label="Drop here...">Having seen his great adversary already feature on this list, it seems fitting that the last word goes to the mercurial Cristiano Ronaldo.</p>                                <div                  id="ad-300x250_LL_m_8"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-300x250 instream-ad mobile-ad "                  data-dimensions="300x250"                  data-tgxtrack="true" data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxupdatecorrelator="true" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                                <div                  id="ad-728x90_LL_td_8"                  class="ad ad-container ad-wrapper type-728x90 instream-ad tablet-ad desktop-ad "                  data-dimensions="728x90"                  data-tgxtargeting="%7B%7D" data-tgxlazy="50"                >                </div>                <p>The Portuguese superstar is widely regarded as a true legend of the game, with his scoring prowess in Spain's La Liga truly staggering. His arrival at Real Madrid in 2009 from Manchester United not only got tongues wagging, but set in motion one of the greatest club careers ever seen.</p>                <p data-label="Drop here...">In just nine seasons, Ronaldo has stormed past the 300 league goals barrier - doing so in just 286 games. Surely another record that will stand the test of time.</p>          </div>        </div>        <!-- Syndication Attribution -->        <!-- Generic Page Content -->        <!-- Bottom Recirc -->
